21b1(2): pa'i bka' 'gyud gras su yed pa'i lag bris yig nag 'phrul dpad can byas pa yin// se rgyun gzhan pa'i bsdud ya ma rnyed pas zhus pes mthong tshed kyis bris pa'i chad lhag dang / mngon gsal can gyi rkyen ma then / 
21b2(2): degs cha brkangs byas na'ang / ma dpe la gang byung gis bces thal la byas// sdung dpen gsas byung ned kyi nye lam sde bzhi' gras su yed pa'i gted 'bum le'u chung de'ang 'did tham bgrigs byas te/ sge bzhi mdzead lnga'i 
21b3(2): / se rnying phyegs bgrigs/ kyo a grangs 1pad zhus bgrigs byas yed kyang ddung ma rtegs dbang gis chad lhag segs yod nges te/ spyi la 2bbyad sngan lo nga lnga brgya lhag nas gangs can gad kyi yul du yi // 
21b4(2): go' par chang 'jugs bskrun dang // se gzhi legs bsgrigs byas pa'i 'grels spel yengs khyab byed srel dad zin na'ang / g.sung dung ben gyi dse gzhi' bsdu bgrigs byed pa'o ga rkabs kyi ched yug de tsam byung med pas/ 
21b5(2): 'did phyegs la nyams myeng dang lag len segs la mig nes len gni dken pas gam cha gsad du yin pa dang / shes su de zhus bgrigs pa che yang mkhyen dpyed dab 'byams pa min chad/ 'di' thad mthun rkyen zung / 
21b6(2): la 'gal rkyen mang ba'i gseb tu dal brling 'grig pa dang ma byung na/ phyegs gang sa'i thad yug dang gnas sangs tshag las brgal ba'i legs cha zhig then thabs med pas/ de lags kyis rjes su gzigs mkhan rnam //
